     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix newsletter_subject" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title--custom-tag afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/958704/what-is-architecture-thoughts-from-yona-friedman-bogdan-and-van-broeck-mad-architects-and-awp-architecture">
        <span itemprop="name">
         What is Architecture? Thoughts from Yona Friedman, Bogdan &amp; Van Broeck, MAD Architects, and AWP Architecture
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <meta content="2021-03-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <!-- / stream date -->
       <span>
        <time data-time-ago="2021-03-21T12:30:00+00:00" datetime="2021-03-21T12:30:00+00:00" lang="en">
         March 21
        </time>
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content" itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6051ef9ef91c81a5e9000262" class="featured-image js-image-size media-picture" data-height="370" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-6051ef9ef91c81a5e9000262" style="width: 640px; height: 370px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/958704/what-is-architecture-thoughts-from-yona-friedman-bogdan-and-van-broeck-mad-architects-and-awp-architecture" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 370px;">
         <img alt="What is Architecture? Thoughts from Yona Friedman, Bogdan &amp; Van Broeck, MAD Architects, and AWP Architecture, Courtesy of What is architecture?" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="6051ef9ef91c81a5e9000262" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6051/ef9e/f91c/81a5/e900/0262/newsletter/WIA_Banner3_2021.jpg?1615982467" data-src-small="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6051/ef9e/f91c/81a5/e900/0262/medium_jpg/WIA_Banner3_2021.jpg?1615982467" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958704/what-is-architecture-thoughts-from-yona-friedman-bogdan-and-van-broeck-mad-architects-and-awp-architecture/6051ef9ef91c81a5e9000262-what-is-architecture-thoughts-from-yona-friedman-bogdan-and-van-broeck-mad-architects-and-awp-architecture-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6051ef9ef91c81a5e9000262">
         Courtesy of What is architecture?
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        Simple in form but complex in substance, “What is Architecture?” remains an existential question for a lot of architecture students and young professionals. In an attempt to define this ever-changing interrogation and expose the different visions out there, the interview series
        <em>
         :
         <a href="https://www.whatisarchitecture.cc/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
          WIA – What is architecture?
         </a>
        </em>
        asks four, straightforward, questions to world-leading architectural designers and thinkers. Seeking to uncover their opinion on what architecture is and what it can do, these short videos reveal responses to “
        <em>
         What is architecture? What can architecture do? What is your architectural position?
        </em>
        and
        <em>
         What is your design method?”
        </em>
        .
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/tag/archdaily-x-wia" target="_blank">
         ArchDaily has collaborated with WIA
        </a>
        to release every week, 4 of these conversations, and to invite you to take on the challenge and answer these questions. The third article of the series presents the ideas and visions of
        <a href="http://www.yonafriedman.nl/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         Yona Friedman
        </a>
        , Oana Bogdan, and Leo Van Broeck from
        <a href="https://www.bogdanvanbroeck.com/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         Bogdan &amp; Van Broeck
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/tag/ma-yansong">
         Ma Yansong
        </a>
        from
        <a href="http://www.i-mad.com/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         MAD Architects
        </a>
        , and Alessandra Cianchetta from
        <a href="https://awp-architecture.com/about?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         AWP Architecture
        </a>
        .
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.com/958704/what-is-architecture-thoughts-from-yona-friedman-bogdan-and-van-broeck-mad-architects-and-awp-architecture
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Christele Harrouk
       </span>
      </div>

      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title--custom-tag afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/958824/alex-proba-on-the-limitation-and-possibilities-of-a-design-style-and-blurring-2d-and-3d-works">
        <span itemprop="name">
         Alex Proba on the Limitation and Possibilities of a Design Style and Blurring 2D and 3D Works
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <meta content="2021-03-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <!-- / stream date -->
       <span>
        <time data-time-ago="2021-03-21T08:30:00+00:00" datetime="2021-03-21T08:30:00+00:00" lang="en">
         March 21
        </time>
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content" itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6053bba7f91c8187aa0005a7" class="featured-image js-image-size media-picture" data-height="335" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-6053bba7f91c8187aa0005a7" style="width: 640px; height: 335px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/958824/alex-proba-on-the-limitation-and-possibilities-of-a-design-style-and-blurring-2d-and-3d-works" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 335px;">
         <img alt="Alex Proba on the Limitation and Possibilities of a Design Style and Blurring 2D and 3D Works, Alex Proba. Image © The Second Studio Podcast" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="6053bba7f91c8187aa0005a7" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6053/bba7/f91c/8187/aa00/05a7/newsletter/The_Second_Podcast_Alex_Proba.jpg?1616100254" data-src-small="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6053/bba7/f91c/8187/aa00/05a7/medium_jpg/The_Second_Podcast_Alex_Proba.jpg?1616100254" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958824/alex-proba-on-the-limitation-and-possibilities-of-a-design-style-and-blurring-2d-and-3d-works/6053bba7f91c8187aa0005a7-alex-proba-on-the-limitation-and-possibilities-of-a-design-style-and-blurring-2d-and-3d-works-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6053bba7f91c8187aa0005a7">
         Alex Proba. Image © The Second Studio Podcast
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        The Second Studio (formerly The Midnight Charette) is an explicit podcast about design, architecture, and the everyday. Hosted by Architects David Lee and Marina Bourderonnet, it features different creative professionals in unscripted conversations that allow for thoughtful takes and personal discussions.
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        A variety of subjects are covered with honesty and humor: some episodes are interviews, while others are tips for fellow designers, reviews of buildings and other projects, or casual explorations of everyday life and design.
        <a href="https://www.secondstudiopod.com/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         The Second Studio
        </a>
        is also available on
        <a href="https://podcasts.apple.com/us/podcast/the-second-studio-design-and-architecture-show/id1223815551?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         iTunes
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="https://open.spotify.com/show/3TVq5fuaZPSzlD84bk3Oqj?si=33AiSsnxSqCZi_yDleaqLA&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         Spotify
        </a>
        , and
        <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCUWyNdjf3Gu6_3gpwq9Yu2Q?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         YouTube
        </a>
        .
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p dir="ltr">
        This week David and Marina are joined by
        <a href="/tag/alex-proba">
         Alex Proba
        </a>
        , Multi-Disciplinary Designer and Creative Director of
        <a href="http://www.studioproba.com/?utm_medium=website&amp;utm_source=archdaily.com" target="_blank">
         Studio Proba
        </a>
        to discuss her design process, finding her own style, the limitation and possibilities of a design style, blurring 2D and 3D works, spatial design, and much more. Enjoy!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="https://www.secondstudiopod.com/">
         <img src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/5fc3/976e/63c0/1711/b900/0076/original/The_Second_Studio_Podcast.jpg?1606653802"/>
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.com/958824/alex-proba-on-the-limitation-and-possibilities-of-a-design-style-and-blurring-2d-and-3d-works
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        The Second Studio Podcast
       </span>
      </div>

          <i class="afd-icon-text__icon afd-icon afd-icon--icon-folder-white">

     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix newsletter_subject" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title--custom-tag afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid">
        <span itemprop="name">
         Uncovering The Hidden Gems Of Brutalism In Madrid
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <meta content="2021-03-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <!-- / stream date -->
       <span>
        <time data-time-ago="2021-03-20T12:30:00+00:00" datetime="2021-03-20T12:30:00+00:00" lang="en">
         March 20
        </time>
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content" itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061" class="featured-image js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="Uncovering The Hidden Gems Of Brutalism In Madrid, Edificio Princesa, residential buildings for the Military Housing Cooperative - Fernando Higueras Díaz, Antonio Miró Valverde and Carlos García Rodríguez. Image © Roberto Conte" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6050/bf50/f91c/81a5/e900/0061/newsletter/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-16.jpg?1615904586" data-src-small="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6050/bf50/f91c/81a5/e900/0061/medium_jpg/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-16.jpg?1615904586" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061">
         Edificio Princesa, residential buildings for the Military Housing Cooperative - Fernando Higueras Díaz, Antonio Miró Valverde and Carlos García Rodríguez. Image © Roberto Conte
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p dir="ltr">
        The city of Madrid can be viewed as a place that is representative of all the architectural styles found on the European continent. 16th-century Renaissance buildings and 18th-century Baroque buildings all co-exist in harmony with more modern architectural styles such as Art Deco or the
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/803314/discover-madrids-geometric-architecture-through-this-photo-series" target="_blank">
         expressive contemporary architecture
        </a>
        of recent years. Iconic contemporary architecture firms such as
        <a href="http://www.archdaily.com/office/herzog-de-meuron" target="_blank">
         Herzog &amp; de Meuron
        </a>
        and
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/office/rogers-stirk-harbour-plus-partners?ad_name=project-specs&amp;ad_medium=single" target="_blank">
         Rogers Stirk Harbour + Partners
        </a>
        , with projects such as the
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/893996/bbva-headquarters-herzog-and-de-meuron" target="_blank">
         BBVA Headquarters
        </a>
        and
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/805964/madrid-barajas-airport-terminal-4-estudio-lamela-plus-richard-rogers-partnership" target="_blank">
         Madrid-Barajas Airport Terminal
        </a>
        , have all played a part in defining Madrid’s architectural character too, making for a city with highly varied and distinct streetscapes.
       </p>
       <p class="thumbs afd-desktop-e clearfix">
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="6050bfb1f91c81a5e9000064" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/6050bfb1f91c81a5e9000064-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Instituto del Patrimonio Cultural de España - Cultural Heritage Institute of Spain - Fernando Higueras Díaz and Antonio Miró Valverde. Image © Roberto Conte" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="6050bfb1f91c81a5e9000064" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6050/bfb1/f91c/81a5/e900/0064/thumb_jpg/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-2.jpg?1615904678" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/6050bfb1f91c81a5e9000064-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="Instituto del Patrimonio Cultural de España - Cultural Heritage Institute of Spain - Fernando Higueras Díaz and Antonio Miró Valverde. Image © Roberto Conte" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="605202f5f91c81a5e9000282" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/605202f5f91c81a5e9000282-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Torres Blancas - Francisco Javier Sáenz de Oíza. Image © Roberto Conte" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="605202f5f91c81a5e9000282" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6052/02f5/f91c/81a5/e900/0282/thumb_jpg/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-4.jpg?1615987438" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/605202f5f91c81a5e9000282-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="Torres Blancas - Francisco Javier Sáenz de Oíza. Image © Roberto Conte" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="605202fcf91c8187aa000242" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/605202fcf91c8187aa000242-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Church of Nuestra Señora del Rosario de Filipinas - Cecilio Sanchez-Robles Tarín. Image © Roberto Conte" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="605202fcf91c8187aa000242" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6052/02fc/f91c/8187/aa00/0242/thumb_jpg/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-5.jpg?1615987445" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.com/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/605202fcf91c8187aa000242-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="Church of Nuestra Señora del Rosario de Filipinas - Cecilio Sanchez-Robles Tarín. Image © Roberto Conte" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="6050bf28f91c8187aa000043" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/6050bf28f91c8187aa000043-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Instituto del Patrimonio Cultural de España - Cultural Heritage Institute of Spain - Fernando Higueras Díaz and Antonio Miró Valverde.         </a>
        <a class="gallery-link afd-desktop-e" href="/958637/uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid/6050bf50f91c81a5e9000061-uncovering-the-hidden-gems-of-brutalism-in-madrid-photo">
         <img class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-src="https://images.adsttc.com/media/images/6050/bf50/f91c/81a5/e900/0061/newsletter/Brutalismo_Madrileno_Roberto_Conte-16.jpg?1615904586" itemprop="image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
         <span class="gallery-link__overlay">

         <span class="gallery-link__content gallery-link__size">
          + 12
         </span>
        </a>
       </p>

      <h3 class="afd-title--custom-tag afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/957036/the-hill-house-maden-group">
        <span itemprop="name">
         The Hill House / Maden GROUP
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <meta content="2021-03-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <!-- / stream date -->
       <span>
        <time data-time-ago="2021-03-20T11:00:00+00:00" datetime="2021-03-20T11:00:00+00:00" lang="en">
         March 20
        </time>
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content" itemprop="articleBody">

  function initializeNotifications() {
    var s, r, t;
    r = false;
    s = document.createElement('script');
    s.type = 'text/javascript';
    s.src = "https://notifications-api.archdaily.com/js/sdk.js";
    s.onload = s.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (!r && (!this.readyState || this.readyState == 'complete')) {
        r = true;
        window.notifications = new NotificationsSDK.default({
          'host': 'https://notifications-api.archdaily.com',
          'myad': 'https://my.archdaily.com'
        });
        window.notifications.setupEntityHints();
        window.notifications.setupButtons();
      }
    };
    t = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
    t.parentNode.insertBefore(s, t);
  }

      }
